Short Name: Chip Overlap vs High Price

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Div($chip_overlap,Sqrt($high))

Compares chip-overlap density with the square-root of the session high. It looks for near-price ownership support that can matter for the next day's move.

Normalizes the `chip_overlap` density metric by the square root of the session high. It assesses the depth of the current order/ownership structure relative to the stock's absolute price level, isolating concentrated nearby stakeholder support configured to defend short-term pullbacks.

Direction: Higher effective score implies stronger near-price positioning support for short-horizon timing.

alpha_0CMANonlinear Volume Dislocation

Index & Meta

Index: 0

Category: CMA

Short Name: Nonlinear Volume Dislocation

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Mul(-1.0,Div($log_volume,Sub(SLog1p(Sub($log_volume,Rank($log_volume))),$log_volume)))

Compares log-volume to a self-referential nonlinear volume baseline. It highlights symbols where participation is unusually strong relative to their own ranked volume regime.

The formula constructs a denominator calculating the difference between a dampened, ranked-adjusted log-volume and the raw log-volume itself. Since the denominator tends to be negative for high volume names, the division yields a negative value, which is then inverted by `Mul(-1.0, ...)` to produce a positive score for actively traded stocks. It isolates local dislocations in trading interest.

Direction: Higher effective score implies unusually strong participation versus local volume baseline.

actionable_alpha_1ACTIONABLERange-Weighted Day Body

Index & Meta

Index: 1

Category: ACTIONABLE

Short Name: Range-Weighted Day Body

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Mul($chl,Sub($close,$open))

Multiplies intraday body (`close-open`) by bar geometry (`chl`). It favors symbols where the day's directional move was backed by meaningful range expansion.

Multiplies the `chl` price geometry metric by the raw intraday cash body (Close - Open). This interaction term strongly magnifies days where positive directional closing momentum is reinforced by a broad intraday range (`chl`), generating a powerful unified continuation signal for the following open.

Direction: Higher effective score implies stronger directional body confirmed by range.

alpha_1CMAMedian Volume Momentum

Index & Meta

Index: 1

Category: CMA

Short Name: Median Volume Momentum

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

TsQuantile(TsMomRank($log_volume,40),0.5,30)

Takes the median rolling quantile of ranked log-volume momentum. It favors names with persistent medium-horizon acceleration in trading activity instead of one-day spikes.

Calculates the rolling 40-day momentum rank of log-volume, then tracks the median (0.5 quantile) of this rank over a 30-day window. This effectively smooths out noisy daily volume spikes, rewarding stocks that have maintained consistently high volume momentum over a medium-term horizon.

Direction: Higher effective score implies steadier positive volume momentum.

actionable_alpha_2ACTIONABLEFFT Momentum vs Chip VWAP

Index & Meta

Index: 2

Category: ACTIONABLE

Short Name: FFT Momentum vs Chip VWAP

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Mul(-1.0,TsCorr(TsNonLinearMom($vol_fft,40),$chip_vwap,15))

Uses the negative correlation between nonlinear FFT momentum and chip VWAP. It seeks names where fast cyclical momentum diverges from chip positioning in a tradable way.

Calculates the 15-day correlation between the 40-day non-linear momentum of cyclical volume (`vol_fft`) and the VWAP of accumulated chips, then inverts the result. It captures an actionable anomaly when rapid high-frequency volume momentum drastically disconnects from the slow-moving ownership basis, setting up explosive short-term adjustments.

Direction: Higher effective score implies a more favorable momentum-versus-positioning divergence.

alpha_2CMAVolume-Price Pressure Quantile

Index & Meta

Index: 2

Category: CMA

Short Name: Volume-Price Pressure Quantile

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

TsQuantile(Sub($log_volume,$log_close),0.67,10)

Measures how much log-volume outruns log-close through an upper-quantile filter. It rewards demand pressure where activity rises faster than price level.

Measures the difference between log-volume and log-close price, approximating the number of shares traded relative to the price level. Taking the 67th percentile (upper tercile) over a fast 10-day window creates a smoothed indicator of sustained demand pressure pushing volume up faster than the stock price appreciates.

Direction: Higher effective score implies stronger volume pressure relative to price level.

Index & Meta

Category: ACTIONABLE

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

TsRelStrength(TsIr($log_volume,30),20,40)

Applies relative strength to the information ratio of log-volume over 30 days. It highlights symbols where participation quality is improving faster than peers across short and medium windows.

Computes the Information Ratio of log volume over 30 days, serving as a participation consistency metric. It then measures the relative strength of a fast 20-day moving average of this IR against a slow 40-day average. This effectively calculates the acceleration of institutional accumulation consistency against its own recent baseline.

Direction: Higher effective score implies stronger relative improvement in volume quality.

alpha_3CMAStress Reversal Correlation

Index & Meta

Index: 3

Category: CMA

Short Name: Stress Reversal Correlation

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Mul(-1.0,TsCorr(Div($log_volume,$open),$low,20))

Uses the negative 20-day correlation between volume/open intensity and lows. It looks for washout patterns where heavy participation coincides with stressed lows that later mean-revert.

Computes the 20-day correlation between open-adjusted volume intensity and the daily low price. The `Mul(-1.0, ...)` operator negates this correlation. A high final score emerges when volume intensity is negatively correlated with lows, indicating heavy accumulation occurring precisely when the price drops, an algorithmic signature of strong mean-reversion support.

Direction: Higher effective score implies healthier reversal support after stress.

actionable_alpha_4ACTIONABLECHL Delta Washout

Index & Meta

Index: 4

Category: ACTIONABLE

Short Name: CHL Delta Washout

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Mul(-1.0,TsQuantile(TsDelta($chl,40),0.25,30))

Takes the negative lower-quantile of 40-day changes in `chl` geometry. It behaves like a washout detector for bar-shape deterioration that can set up short-horizon reversals.

First tracks the 40-day change (`TsDelta`) in `chl` gap geometry, then isolates the 25th percentile path of those changes over 30 days. The `-1.0` multiplier converts the most severe, chronic deteriorations in bar shape into high scores, generating a potent mean-reversion buy signal based on extreme structural washout.

Direction: Higher effective score implies a more washed-out recent geometry profile.

alpha_4CMAFFT Liquidity Stress

Index & Meta

Index: 4

Category: CMA

Short Name: FFT Liquidity Stress

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Mul(-1.0,Div(TsRank($vol_fft,40),$amihud_mean))

Penalizes high FFT-ranked activity when Amihud liquidity is poor. It surfaces names with strong cyclic activity but still acceptable microstructure quality.

Divides the rolling 40-day rank of the spectral volume signature (vol_fft) by the Amihud illiquidity mean. Because Amihud gets larger when liquidity is worse, strong cyclical activity coupled with excellent liquidity creates a huge positive value, which the outermost `Mul(-1.0, ...)` flips into a highly negative score. The score serves as an inverted quality measure where lower (more negative) values indicate optimal liquid cyclic activity.

Direction: Higher effective score implies stronger activity after adjusting for liquidity cost.

Index & Meta

Index: 5

Category: ACTIONABLE

Short Name: Break-Revert Momentum Burst

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Sqrt(Abs(TsNonLinearMom($high_break_revert_45_5,20)))

Uses the square-root magnitude of nonlinear momentum in the `high_break_revert_45_5` feature. It searches for actionable bursts in breakout-then-reversion behavior.

Takes the 20-day non-linear (third central) moment of a specific breakout-reversion feature (`high_break_revert_45_5`). By taking the absolute value and square root, it strictly flags any magnitude burst in this non-linear dynamic behavior, signaling high short-term volatility or imminent tactical shifts regardless of immediate direction.

Direction: Higher effective score implies a stronger short-horizon break-revert signal.

alpha_5CMACapital Flow Intensity

Index & Meta

Index: 5

Category: CMA

Short Name: Capital Flow Intensity

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Div($log_money,Sub($log_money,$ohl))

Scales log-money by the gap between log-money and intraday range geometry (`ohl`). It seeks names where traded capital is large relative to price-spread structure.

Scales logarithmic dollar volume by the difference between itself and the `ohl` gap metric. This highlights periods where the absolute capital flowing into a stock fundamentally dwarfs its intraday structural price variance, indicating strong institutional sponsorship holding down volatility relative to trading magnitude.

Direction: Higher effective score implies stronger capital-flow support.

alpha_6CMAHigh-to-VWAP Location

Index & Meta

Index: 6

Category: CMA

Short Name: High-to-VWAP Location

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Rank(Div(Sqrt($high),$vwap))

Ranks the ratio of sqrt(high) to VWAP. It acts like a price-location quality measure, favoring names trading closer to their session highs versus average execution level.

Ranks the ratio of the square root of the high price to the VWAP across the cross-section. The square root transformation dampens extreme high prints. High ranks are achieved by stocks pushing consistently higher trading ranges and execution volumes well above their average weighted execution price, signaling robust intraday buying control.

Direction: Higher effective score implies better price-location quality around the high.

actionable_alpha_7ACTIONABLEInverted Gap Compression

Index & Meta

Index: 7

Category: ACTIONABLE

Short Name: Inverted Gap Compression

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Mul(-1.0,SLog1p(Div(Rank($ohl),$chlo)))

Negates a smoothed log transform of ranked `ohl/chlo` geometry. It looks for compressed or distorted gap structure that may unwind over the next day.

Constructs a ratio of cross-sectionally ranked `ohl` geometry against `chlo`, logging the result and negating it. This inverted logarithmic compression signals a distorted, unusually squashed daily bar structure compared to peers, frequently acting as a coil or spring anticipating violent directional expansion.

Direction: Higher effective score implies a more favorable compression or reset pattern.

alpha_7CMAFlow Volatility Quantile

Index & Meta

Index: 7

Category: CMA

Short Name: Flow Volatility Quantile

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

TsQuantile(TsMad($log_money,20),0.33,10)

Uses a lower quantile of the rolling MAD of log-money. It looks for regimes where capital-flow dispersion is informative without being explosively unstable.

Calculates the 20-day mean absolute deviation (MAD) of capital flows (log-money), then takes a lower tercile (0.33 quantile) over 10 days. This extracts stocks entering a regime of constricted capital flow volatility, pointing towards a consolidation phase where structural pricing shifts happen without chaotic money rotation, providing a stable baseline.

Direction: Higher effective score implies a more favorable flow-volatility regime.

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Mul(-1.0,TsRelStrength($ohl,20,30))

Applies negative relative strength to `ohl` geometry. It is a contrarian short-horizon setup that prefers names where this bar-structure measure has recently weakened versus peers.

Computes a moving average crossover relative strength (20-day vs 30-day) on the standalone `ohl` gap feature and multiplies by -1.0. This scores highest when the 20-day trend of the `ohl` structure begins meaningfully underperforming its 30-day average, signaling an actionable contrarian entry point.

Direction: Higher effective score implies more attractive contrarian weakness in `ohl` structure.

Category: CMA

Short Name: Microstructure Confirmation Stack

Expr & Interpretation

Add(Add($amihud_mean,TsCorr($vwap,$chip_vwap,15)),Add(Abs(Sub($chlo,SLog1p($amihud_range))),Add(Rank($chlo),Add($chlo,$ohlc))))

Adds Amihud level, VWAP-chip correlation, and several gap-geometry terms into a broad confirmation factor. It rewards names where liquidity, chip positioning, and price structure all point the same way.

alpha_10CMAOpen Return Rebound Quantile

Index & Meta

Index: 10

Category: CMA

Short Name: Open Return Rebound Quantile

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Mul(-1.0,TsQuantile(Ret($open),0.25,40))

Takes the negative lower-quantile of open returns over 40 days. It is an oversold-rebound factor that favors names with sufficiently washed-out recent opening moves.

Captures the 25th percentile (lower quartile) of daily open returns over a 40-day window, measuring the worst characteristic morning drops. Multiplying by -1.0 transforms severe negative open paths into high positive scores, acting as an oversold rebound trigger targeting stocks exhibiting washed-out opening plunge exhaustion.

Direction: Higher effective score implies a more attractive open-driven rebound setup.

actionable_alpha_11ACTIONABLEInverse Drift Relative Weakness

Index & Meta

Index: 11

Category: ACTIONABLE

Short Name: Inverse Drift Relative Weakness

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Mul(-1.0,TsRelStrength(Inv($drift_factor),10,30))

Applies negative relative strength to the inverse drift factor. In practice it favors names where the 'bad drift' regime is losing strength rather than accelerating.

Calculates the relative strength of the inverse drift factor (10-day vs 30-day) and negates it. Because drift is inverted first, a weakening of this inverse (less bad drift) creates a negative relative strength. The `-1.0` turns this into a positive score, perfectly highlighting stocks where toxic intraday behavior is successfully decaying.

Direction: Higher effective score implies improving drift conditions for next-day timing.

alpha_11CMAVolume Dispersion MAD

Index & Meta

Index: 11

Category: CMA

Short Name: Volume Dispersion MAD

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

TsMad($log_volume,30)

Uses the rolling MAD of log-volume to capture abnormal participation dispersion. It tends to flag names where crowding or neglect is becoming informative.

Computes the 30-day Mean Absolute Deviation of log volume. This pure dispersion metric identifies symbols experiencing unusually fragmented or dispersed participation (abnormal volume). Elevated levels frequently precede regime shifts, as stable neglect or steady crowding gives way to disagreement and eventual breakout or breakdown.

Direction: Higher effective score implies a more favorable abnormal-volume regime.

actionable_alpha_12ACTIONABLEAmihud Range Compression

Index & Meta

Index: 12

Category: ACTIONABLE

Short Name: Amihud Range Compression

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Mul(-1.0,Inv(TsRelStrength($amihud_range,10,15)))

Negates the inverse of short-term relative strength in Amihud range. It prefers names where liquidity stress is compressing or easing instead of getting worse.

Evaluates short-term Easing of liquidity stress. A negative relative strength shows 10-day amihud range underperforming 15-day range (improving liquidity). Its inverse becomes a large negative structural value, which is then flipped positive by `Mul(-1.0, ...)`. It mathematically guarantees the highest score for the most radically improving short-term liquidity profiles.

Direction: Higher effective score implies improving short-term liquidity stress.

alpha_12CMAPrice vs Chip Support Correlation

Index & Meta

Index: 12

Category: CMA

Short Name: Price vs Chip Support Correlation

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

Sub($ohlc,TsCorr($volume,$chip_near_support,10))

Subtracts volume-to-chip-support correlation from `ohlc` gap geometry. It prefers names whose price structure remains strong even as chip-near-support dynamics shift.

Subtracts the 10-day short-term correlation between raw volume and near-support chip density from the `ohlc` gap geometry. High scores occur when a stock demonstrates structurally strong bar profiles (`ohlc`) simultaneously diverging from the reliance on immediate volume-driven support, suggesting self-sustaining price momentum.

Direction: Higher effective score implies supportive price structure relative to chip-support behavior.

actionable_alpha_13ACTIONABLE30d Break-Revert Rank Return

Index & Meta

Index: 13

Category: ACTIONABLE

Short Name: 30d Break-Revert Rank Return

Data Date: 2026-03-17

Expr & Interpretation

TsRet(Rank($high_break_revert_45_5),30)

Takes the 30-day return of the ranked `high_break_revert_45_5` feature. It captures whether breakout-revert leadership itself is trending up or down.

Derives a 30-day momentum (return) strictly on the cross-sectional rank of the breakout-revert metric, rather than price. This acts as a meta-trend indicator, prioritizing stocks currently riding a powerful uptrend in their own systematic breakout-reversion characteristic behavior across the market breadth.

Direction: Higher effective score implies stronger recent performance of the break-revert rank signal.
